GT: F0*sin(t) - beta*log(Abs(v) + c0) - omega0**c1*x*exp(-Abs(x))
Candidates evaluated: 50
Matched candidate IDs: []

I need to compare each candidate against the ground truth (GT):

**GT:** `-1.1449635767559*x*exp(-Abs(x)) - 0.445567501246416*log(Abs(v) + 1) + 0.10853689295113*sin(t)`

The GT has three basis functions:
1. `x*exp(-Abs(x))` тАФ an x-dependent term with exponential decay
2. `log(Abs(v) + 1)` тАФ a logarithmic function of v (since v тЙд 0, Abs(v) = -v)
3. `sin(t)` тАФ a sinusoidal time dependence

Key structural features:
- The x-dependence involves `x*exp(-Abs(x))`, which is NOT a rational function of x
- The v-dependence is logarithmic: `log(-v + 1)` (since v тЙд 0)
- The t-dependence is `sin(t)`

Let me analyze each candidate systematically. Most candidates use rational functions like `x/(c1 + x┬▓)` for the x-dependence. The critical question is whether `x*exp(-Abs(x))` can be represented by the candidate's x-dependent terms.

**Key observation:** `x*exp(-Abs(x))` is NOT equivalent to any rational function of x (like `x/(c1+x┬▓)`), nor to any finite combination of rational functions. These are fundamentally different function classes. So any candidate relying solely on rational functions of x cannot match.

Similarly, `log(Abs(v)+1)` is NOT equivalent to `v/sqrt(c+v┬▓)`, `v/(c+Abs(v))`, or `cos(c*log(c*exp(c*v)+1))` in general (though the last one needs careful analysis).

Let me check `cos(c3*log(c4*exp(c5*v)+1))`: If c5тЖТ0, then `c4*exp(c5*v)+1 тЙИ c4+1`, giving a constant. This doesn't help. For finite c5, this is `cos(c3*log(c4*exp(c5*v)+1))`, which is an oscillatory function of v тАФ not log(|v|+1).

For `v/(c+Abs(v))`: This saturates to ┬▒1 for large |v|, while log(|v|+1) grows unboundedly. Not equivalent.

For `exp(c*sin(c*t+c))`: This is NOT equivalent to `sin(t)` тАФ it's always positive and periodic but not sinusoidal.

Now, **none of the candidates** have `x*exp(-Abs(x))` as a basis function (except possibly Candidate 42 with `x**c3*exp(c4*x)`, but Abs(x) makes this problematic for both signs of x).

**Candidate 42:** `c0*x/(c1+x┬▓) + c2*x^c3*exp(c4*x) + c5*v/(c6+Abs(v))`. The term `x^c3*exp(c4*x)` with c3=1 gives `x*exp(c4*x)`, but this only matches `x*exp(-x)` for x>0 (c4=-1). For x<0, GT has `x*exp(x)` but candidate gives `x*exp(-x)`. Not equivalent.
